province_event = { #SECRET MAJORITY
	id = AN_culture_matrix.5
	title = "AN_culture_matrix.5.t"
	desc = "AN_culture_matrix.5.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#AN_check_dev_variables = yes
			set_ttt_bar_data = {
				bg=yes
				id=3
				size=M
				color=3 #for red, 3 for blue
				data=AN_culture_progress
				datatype=which
				max=100
				maxtype=value
				min=0
				mintype=value
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #culture becomes target - for parent and national cultures
		name = "AN_culture_matrix.integrate_maj"
		trigger = { accepted_culture = ROOT }
		AN_integrate_majority_culture = yes
		province_event = { id = AN_culture_matrix.5 days = 0 }
	}

	option = { #culture becomes accepted
		name = "AN_culture_matrix.accept_maj"
		trigger = { NOT = { accepted_culture = ROOT } }
		AN_accept_majority_culture = yes
		province_event = { id = AN_culture_matrix.5 days = 0 }
	}

	option = { #reduce non-accepted malus
		name = "AN_culture_matrix.suppress_maj"
		trigger = { NOT = { accepted_culture = ROOT } }
		AN_suppress_majority_culture = yes
		province_event = { id = AN_culture_matrix.5 days = 0 }
	}


	option = { #back
		name = "setup.back"
		owner = { country_event = { id = AN_culture_matrix.1 days = 0 } }
	}
	option = { #exit
		name = "setup.exit"
	}
}

province_event = { #SECRET MINORITY
	id = AN_culture_matrix.6
	title = "AN_culture_matrix.6.t"
	desc = "AN_culture_matrix.6.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#AN_check_dev_variables = yes
			set_ttt_bar_data = {
				bg=yes
				id=3
				size=M
				color=3 #for red, 3 for blue
				data=AN_culture_progress
				datatype=which
				max=100
				maxtype=value
				min=0
				mintype=value
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #culture becomes target - for parent and national cultures
		name = "AN_culture_matrix.integrate_min"
		trigger = { OR = { has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_1 has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_2 has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_3 } }
		AN_integrate_minority_culture = yes
		province_event = { id = AN_culture_matrix.6 days = 0 }
	}

	option = { #culture becomes accepted
		name = "AN_culture_matrix.integrate_min"
		trigger = { NOT = { OR = { has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_1 has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_2 has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_3 has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_1 has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_2 has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_3 } } }
		AN_accept_minority_culture = yes
		province_event = { id = AN_culture_matrix.6 days = 0 }
	}

	option = { #reduce non-accepted malus - slow emigration
		name = "AN_culture_matrix.suppress_min"
		trigger = { NOT = { OR = { has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_1 has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_2 has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_3 has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_1 has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_2 has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_3 } } }
		AN_suppress_minority_culture = yes
		province_event = { id = AN_culture_matrix.6 days = 0 }
	}



	option = { #back
		name = "setup.back"
		owner = { country_event = { id = AN_culture_matrix.1 days = 0 } }
	}
	option = { #exit
		name = "setup.exit"
	}
}
